    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [q0]
LEFT JOIN [Topics] AS [t] ON [q0].[TopicId] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [AnswerOptions] AS [a] ON [q0].[Id] = [a].[QuestionId]
ORDER BY [q0].[Id], [t].[Id]
